{Piazhai/Pilai means blame/fault, not responsibility. Poruppu means responsibility. There is a difference between 'you are responsible' and 'you are to blame'. If a flood happens at Chennai, the CM is not to blame as they did not cause the flood themselves. But the CM is indeed responsible for the situation in that he has to take care of whatever happens and more importantly, take steps to prevent or treat the damage. When a relationship hasn't even begun yet, blaming a woman as responsible for the feelings that you have, is not correct. The tamil is correct, un mel thaan pizhai, she indeed caused the feelings in him. But she is not responsible for those feelings, he is to be held responsible. Avan mel pizhai illai, anaal avan mazhai mel poruppu avanathe, avazhuthu kadaiyathu. This is a translation error in the script of movie, ultimately. I am of course, talking about 1:13}

{If memory is right, the movie was released around November 15 2008. However, as with my case of all fine things coming to life only a bit late, I heard this song for the 1st time on 14/11/2009, exactly 1 year later. It was on a stormy drive to  Thirunelveli that this song came into my notice. It was a mad drive, with the strom pounding the coastal belt from Kanyakumari to Thirunelveli. With the rain pounding so hard onto the roof of car, the music was barely audible, but even through all that commotion, this melody just soothed. Maybe, its the catch word of 'mazhai' that got the song to my notice. Still wonder why it took 1 year for the song to come to my notice or 'Ennodu va veedu varaikkum' or to rephrase, "Enoodu vaa en idhayam varaikkum". It hasn't left ever since.}
